
============== high level task decomposition ================
[{'objective': 'Represent rectangles ABCD and EFGH with given side lengths and assign coordinates to their vertices.'}, {'objective': 'Use the collinearity of points D, E, C, and F to establish relationships between their coordinates or segment lengths.'}, {'objective': 'Apply the cyclic quadrilateral condition on points A, D, H, and G to derive additional geometric constraints.'}, {'objective': 'Combine all geometric constraints and solve the resulting equations to find the length of segment CE.'}]
============== task analysis ================
1. Extract and Summarize Given Information:
- Two rectangles named ABCD and EFGH are given.
- Points D, E, C, and F are collinear, meaning these four points lie on a single straight line.
- Points A, D, H, and G lie on the same circle, indicating these four points are concyclic.
- Side lengths are provided: BC = 16, AB = 107 for rectangle ABCD; FG = 17, EF = 184 for rectangle EFGH.
- The problem asks for the length of segment CE.

Properties:
- ABCD and EFGH are rectangles, so all angles are right angles, and opposite sides are equal.
- The given side lengths correspond to adjacent sides of the rectangles.
- The concyclicity of A, D, H, G imposes a circle passing through these four points.

2. Analyze Relationships Between Components:
- Since ABCD and EFGH are rectangles, their sides are perpendicular and lengths are fixed by given values.
- The collinearity of D, E, C, F suggests a linear alignment that connects points from both rectangles.
- The concyclicity of A, D, H, G links points from both rectangles on a common circle, imposing geometric constraints.
- The given side lengths define the scale and orientation of the rectangles.
- The segment CE connects a vertex from ABCD (C) to a vertex from EFGH (E), and its length is to be found.
- The conditions likely restrict the relative positioning of the rectangles and the points, influencing CE.

3. Identify the Field of Study:
- The problem lies in Euclidean Geometry, specifically planar geometry involving polygons and circles.
- Subfields include properties of rectangles, concyclic points (circle geometry), and collinearity.
- Such problems are common in mathematical competitions and geometric problem solving.

4. Highlight Aspects Needing Clarification:
- The exact orientation and relative positioning of the rectangles are not explicitly stated.
- It is unclear how the rectangles are placed with respect to each other beyond the given collinearity and concyclicity conditions.
- The order of points on the circle and line is not specified, which may affect interpretation.
- Without coordinate or angle information, multiple configurations might satisfy the given conditions.
- The problem assumes standard rectangle properties but does not specify which sides correspond to which points beyond the given lengths.
============== task decomposition 0 ================
{'stage_0': {'subtask_1': {'objective': 'Derive coordinate or vector representations for rectangles ABCD and EFGH using given side lengths and rectangle properties, and represent points D, E, C, F, A, H, G accordingly.', 'dependencies': [], 'agent_collaboration': 'SC_CoT'}, 'subtask_2': {'objective': 'Formulate the geometric constraints of collinearity (D, E, C, F) and concyclicity (A, D, H, G) in terms of the derived representations.', 'dependencies': ['subtask_1'], 'agent_collaboration': 'SC_CoT'}}, 'stage_1': {'subtask_3': {'objective': 'Identify and verify the relative positioning and orientation of the rectangles that satisfy both the collinearity and concyclicity constraints, ensuring uniqueness or compatibility of the configuration.', 'dependencies': ['stage_0.subtask_2'], 'agent_collaboration': 'Debate'}}, 'stage_2': {'subtask_4': {'objective': 'Decompose the segment CE into components or expressions based on the established configuration, simplifying the expression for CE using known lengths and geometric relations.', 'dependencies': ['stage_1.subtask_3'], 'agent_collaboration': 'Reflexion'}}, 'stage_3': {'subtask_5': {'objective': 'Aggregate and combine the simplified components or expressions to compute the numeric length of segment CE.', 'dependencies': ['stage_0.subtask_1', 'stage_2.subtask_4'], 'agent_collaboration': 'SC_CoT'}}}
============== code generate 0 ================
async def forward(self, taskInfo):
    from collections import Counter
    print("Task Requirement: ", taskInfo)
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    cot_sc_instruction_1 = "Sub-task 1: Derive coordinate or vector representations for rectangles ABCD and EFGH using given side lengths and rectangle properties, and represent points D, E, C, F, A, H, G accordingly, based on the query." 
    N = self.max_sc
    cot_agents_1 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N)]
    possible_answers_1 = []
    possible_thinkings_1 = []
    subtask_desc1 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_1,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N):
        thinking1, answer1 = await cot_agents_1[i]([taskInfo], cot_sc_instruction_1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_1[i].id}, derive coordinates and point representations, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")
        possible_answers_1.append(answer1)
        possible_thinkings_1.append(thinking1)
    final_decision_agent_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking1, answer1 = await final_decision_agent_1([taskInfo] + possible_thinkings_1 + possible_answers_1, "Sub-task 1: Synthesize and choose the most consistent coordinate and point representation for rectangles and points.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}")
    subtask_desc1['response'] = {"thinking": thinking1, "answer": answer1}
    logs.append(subtask_desc1)
    print("Step 1: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_sc_instruction_2 = "Sub-task 2: Formulate the geometric constraints of collinearity (D, E, C, F) and concyclicity (A, D, H, G) in terms of the derived coordinate representations from Sub-task 1." 
    cot_agents_2 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N)]
    possible_answers_2 = []
    possible_thinkings_2 = []
    subtask_desc2 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_2",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_2,
        "context": ["user query", thinking1, answer1],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N):
        thinking2, answer2 = await cot_agents_2[i]([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1], cot_sc_instruction_2, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_2[i].id}, formulate geometric constraints, thinking: {thinking2.content}; answer: {answer2.content}")
        possible_answers_2.append(answer2)
        possible_thinkings_2.append(thinking2)
    final_decision_agent_2 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking2, answer2 = await final_decision_agent_2([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1] + possible_thinkings_2 + possible_answers_2, "Sub-task 2: Synthesize and choose the most consistent geometric constraints formulation.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking2.content}; answer - {answer2.content}")
    subtask_desc2['response'] = {"thinking": thinking2, "answer": answer2}
    logs.append(subtask_desc2)
    print("Step 2: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    debate_instr_3 = "Sub-task 3: Identify and verify the relative positioning and orientation of the rectangles that satisfy both the collinearity and concyclicity constraints, ensuring uniqueness or compatibility of the configuration. Given solutions to the problem from other agents, consider their opinions as additional advice. Please think carefully and provide an updated answer."
    debate_agents_3 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Debate Agent", model=self.node_model, role=role, temperature=0.5) for role in self.debate_role]
    N_max_3 = self.max_round
    all_thinking3 = [[] for _ in range(N_max_3)]
    all_answer3 = [[] for _ in range(N_max_3)]
    subtask_desc3 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_3",
        "instruction": debate_instr_3,
        "context": ["user query", thinking2, answer2],
        "agent_collaboration": "Debate"
    }
    for r in range(N_max_3):
        for i, agent in enumerate(debate_agents_3):
            if r == 0:
                thinking3, answer3 = await agent([taskInfo, thinking2, answer2], debate_instr_3, r, is_sub_task=True)
            else:
                input_infos_3 = [taskInfo, thinking2, answer2] + all_thinking3[r-1] + all_answer3[r-1]
                thinking3, answer3 = await agent(input_infos_3, debate_instr_3, r, is_sub_task=True)
            agents.append(f"Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, verifying configuration, thinking: {thinking3.content}; answer: {answer3.content}")
            all_thinking3[r].append(thinking3)
            all_answer3[r].append(answer3)
    final_decision_agent_3 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking3, answer3 = await final_decision_agent_3([taskInfo, thinking2, answer2] + all_thinking3[-1] + all_answer3[-1], "Sub-task 3: Final decision on configuration verification.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3 output: thinking - {thinking3.content}; answer - {answer3.content}")
    subtask_desc3['response'] = {"thinking": thinking3, "answer": answer3}
    logs.append(subtask_desc3)
    print("Step 3: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    reflect_inst_4 = "Given previous attempts and feedback, carefully consider where you could go wrong in your latest attempt. Using insights from previous attempts, try to solve the task better."
    cot_reflect_instruction_4 = "Sub-task 4: Decompose the segment CE into components or expressions based on the established configuration, simplifying the expression for CE using known lengths and geometric relations." + reflect_inst_4
    cot_agent_4 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_4 = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_4 = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_4 = [taskInfo, thinking3, answer3]
    subtask_desc4 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_4",
        "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction_4,
        "context": ["user query", thinking3, answer3],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }
    thinking4, answer4 = await cot_agent_4(cot_inputs_4, cot_reflect_instruction_4, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_4.id}, decompose and simplify CE, thinking: {thinking4.content}; answer: {answer4.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_4):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent_4([taskInfo, thinking4, answer4], "Please review and provide the limitations of provided solutions. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_4.id}, feedback: {feedback.content}; correct: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_4.extend([thinking4, answer4, feedback])
        thinking4, answer4 = await cot_agent_4(cot_inputs_4, cot_reflect_instruction_4, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_4.id}, refining CE decomposition, thinking: {thinking4.content}; answer: {answer4.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 4 output: thinking - {thinking4.content}; answer - {answer4.content}")
    subtask_desc4['response'] = {"thinking": thinking4, "answer": answer4}
    logs.append(subtask_desc4)
    print("Step 4: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_sc_instruction_5 = "Sub-task 5: Aggregate and combine the simplified components or expressions to compute the numeric length of segment CE, based on outputs from Sub-task 1 and Sub-task 4." 
    cot_agents_5 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N)]
    possible_answers_5 = []
    possible_thinkings_5 = []
    subtask_desc5 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_5",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_5,
        "context": ["user query", thinking1, answer1, thinking4, answer4],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N):
        thinking5, answer5 = await cot_agents_5[i]([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking4, answer4], cot_sc_instruction_5, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_5[i].id}, compute numeric length of CE, thinking: {thinking5.content}; answer: {answer5.content}")
        possible_answers_5.append(answer5)
        possible_thinkings_5.append(thinking5)
    final_decision_agent_5 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking5, answer5 = await final_decision_agent_5([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking4, answer4] + possible_thinkings_5 + possible_answers_5, "Sub-task 5: Synthesize and choose the most consistent numeric length of CE.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5 output: thinking - {thinking5.content}; answer - {answer5.content}")
    subtask_desc5['response'] = {"thinking": thinking5, "answer": answer5}
    logs.append(subtask_desc5)
    print("Step 5: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking5, answer5, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs

async def forward(self, taskInfo):
    from collections import Counter
    print("Task Requirement: ", taskInfo)
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    cot_sc_instruction_1 = (
        "Sub-task 1: Derive coordinate representations for rectangles ABCD and EFGH using the given side lengths and rectangle properties. "
        "Explicitly consider both possible orientations (above and below the reference line) for segment FG to preserve sign choices for points H and G. "
        "Represent points A, B, C, D, E, F, G, H accordingly, setting up a coordinate system that facilitates algebraic manipulation."
    )
    cot_sc_agents_1 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(self.max_sc)]
    possible_answers_1 = []
    possible_thinkings_1 = []
    subtask_desc_1 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_1,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(self.max_sc):
        thinking1, answer1 = await cot_sc_agents_1[i]([taskInfo], cot_sc_instruction_1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_sc_agents_1[i].id}, deriving coordinates, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")
        possible_answers_1.append(answer1)
        possible_thinkings_1.append(thinking1)
    final_decision_agent_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking1, answer1 = await final_decision_agent_1([taskInfo] + possible_thinkings_1 + possible_answers_1, 
                                                    "Sub-task 1: Synthesize and choose the most consistent coordinate setup for rectangles ABCD and EFGH.", 
                                                    is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}")
    subtask_desc_1['response'] = {"thinking": thinking1, "answer": answer1}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_1)
    print("Step 1: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    N_max_4 = self.max_round

        feedback, correct = await critic_agent_4([taskInfo, thinking4, answer4], 
                                               "Please review the answer above and criticize on where might be wrong. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", 
                                               i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_4.id}, providing feedback, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_4.extend([thinking4, answer4, feedback])
        thinking4, answer4 = await cot_agent_4(cot_inputs_4, reflect_instruction_4, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_4.id}, refining length CE, thinking: {thinking4.content}; answer: {answer4.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 4 output: thinking - {thinking4.content}; answer - {answer4.content}")
    subtask_desc_4['response'] = {"thinking": thinking4, "answer": answer4}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_4)
    print("Step 4: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_sc_instruction_5 = (
        "Sub-task 5: Aggregate and compute the numeric length of segment CE using the simplified expression from Sub-task 4. "
        "Perform consistency checks against all problem constraints (rectangle properties, collinearity, concyclicity) to confirm the correctness of the solution. "
        "Provide a fully justified final numeric answer with detailed reasoning and validation."
    )

    possible_answers_5 = []
    possible_thinkings_5 = []
    subtask_desc_5 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_5",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_5,
        "context": ["user query", thinking4, answer4, thinking3, answer3],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(self.max_sc):
        thinking5, answer5 = await cot_sc_agents_5[i]([taskInfo, thinking4, answer4, thinking3, answer3], cot_sc_instruction_5, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_sc_agents_5[i].id}, computing and verifying CE, thinking: {thinking5.content}; answer: {answer5.content}")
